    31	  dark?: string

    34	export interface PreflightsTheme {
    35	  /**
    36	   * Generate theme keys as CSS variables.
    37	   *
    38	   * - `true`: Generate theme keys fully.
    39	   * - `false`: Disable theme keys. (Not recommended ⚠️)
    40	   * - `'on-demand'`: Generate theme keys only when used.
    41	   *
    42	   * @default 'on-demand'
    43	   */
    44	  mode?: boolean | 'on-demand'
    45	
    46	  /**
    47	   * Process the theme keys.
    48	   */
    49	  process?: Arrayable<(entry: CSSEntry, ctx: PreflightContext<Theme>) => void>
    50	}

    53	  /**

    55	   *
    56	   * @default 'class'
    57	   */
    58	  dark?: 'class' | 'media' | DarkModeSelectors
    59	
    60	  /**
    61	   * Generate tagged pseudo selector as `[group=""]` instead of `.group`
    62	   *
    63	   * @default false

    65	  attributifyPseudo?: boolean
    66

    73

    75	   * Utils prefix. When using tagged pseudo selector, only the first truthy prefix will be used.
    76	   *
    77	   * @default undefined
    78	   */
    79	  prefix?: string | string[]
    80	
    81	  /**
    82	   * Enable arbitrary variants, for example `<div class="[&>*]:m-1 [&[open]]:p-2"></div>`.
    83	   *
    84	   * Disable this might slightly improve the performance.
    85	   *
    86	   * @default true
    87	   */
    88	  arbitraryVariants?: boolean
    89	
    90	  /**
    91	   * The important option lets you control whether UnoCSS’s utilities should be marked with `!important`.
    92	   *
    93	   * This can be really useful when using UnoCSS with existing CSS that has high specificity selectors.
    94	   *
    95	   * You can also set `important` to a selector like `#app` instead, which will generate `#app :is(.m-1) { ... }`
    96	   *
    97	   * Also check out the compatibility with [:is()](https://caniuse.com/?search=%3Ais())
    98	   *
    99	   * @default false
   100	   */
   101	  important?: boolean | string
   102	
   103	  /**
   104	   * Control the preflight styles.
   105	   */
   106	  preflights?: {
   107	    /**
   108	     * Reset the default preflight styles.
   109	     *
   110	     * @default true
   111	     */
   112	    reset?: boolean
   113	
   114	    /**
   115	     * Theme configuration for preflight styles.
   116	     *

   118	     *
   119	     * The theme defines the base styles applied to elements and can be customized

   121	     */
   122	    theme?: PreflightsTheme['mode'] | PreflightsTheme
   123	  }
   124	}
   125	
   126	export const presetWind4 = definePreset<PresetWind4Options, Theme>((options = {}) => {
   127	  options.dark = options.dark ?? 'class'
   128	  options.attributifyPseudo = options.attributifyPseudo ?? false
   129	  options.variablePrefix = options.variablePrefix ?? 'un-'
   130	  options.important = options.important ?? false
   131	
   132	  const preflightsTheme = (typeof options.preflights?.theme === 'boolean' || typeof options.preflights?.theme === 'string')
   133	    ? { mode: options.preflights.theme ?? 'on-demand' }
   134	    : { mode: options.preflights?.theme?.mode ?? 'on-demand', ...options.preflights?.theme }
   135	
   136	  options.preflights = {
   137	    reset: options.preflights?.reset ?? true,
   138	    theme: preflightsTheme,
   139	  }
   140	
   141	  return {
   142	    name: PRESET_NAME,
   143	    rules,
   144	    shortcuts,
   145	    theme,
   146	    layers: {
   147	      properties: -200,
   148	      theme: -150,
   149	      base: -100,
   150	    },
   151	    preflights: preflights(options),
   152	    variants: variants(options),
   153	    prefix: options.prefix,
   154	    postprocess: postprocessors(options),
   155	    extractorDefault: options.arbitraryVariants === false
   156	      ? undefined
   157	      : extractorArbitraryVariants(),
   158	    autocomplete: {
   159	      shorthands,
   160	    },
   161	    options,
   162	    configResolved() {
   163	      trackedTheme.clear()
   164	      trackedProperties.clear()
   165	    },
   166	    meta: {
   167	      themeDeps: trackedTheme,
   168	      propertyDeps: trackedProperties,
   169	    },
   170	  }
   171	})
   172	
   173	export default presetWind4

Here's the result of running `cat -n` on /testbed/packages-presets/preset-wind4/src/postprocess/important.ts:
     1	import type { Postprocessor } from '@unocss/core'
     2	import type { PresetWind4Options } from '..'
     3	
     4	export function important({ important: option }: PresetWind4Options): Postprocessor[] {
     5	  if (option == null || option === false)
     6	    return []
     7	
     8	  const wrapWithIs = (selector: string) => {
     9	    if (selector.startsWith(':is(') && selector.endsWith(')'))
    10	      return selector
    11	
    12	    // handle pseudo
    13	    if (selector.includes('::'))
    14	      return selector.replace(/(.*?)((?:\s\*)?::.*)/, ':is($1)$2')
    15	
    16	    return `:is(${selector})`
    17	  }
    18	
    19	  return [
    20	    option === true
    21	      ? (util) => {
    22	          // If the util is a property layer, we should not add `!important` to it
    23	          if (util.layer === 'properties')
    24	            return
    25	
    26	          util.entries.forEach((i) => {
    27	            if (i[1] != null && !String(i[1]).endsWith('!important'))
    28	              i[1] += ' !important'
    29	          })
    30	        }
    31	      : (util) => {
    32	          if (!util.selector.startsWith(option))
    33	            util.selector = `${option} ${wrapWithIs(util.selector)}`
    34	        },
    35	  ]
    36	}
    37

     1	import type { Postprocessor } from '@unocss/core'
     2	import type { PresetWind4Options } from '..'
     3	
     4	export function varPrefix({ variablePrefix: prefix }: PresetWind4Options): Postprocessor[] {
     5	  const processor: Postprocessor = (obj) => {
     6	    obj.entries.forEach((i) => {
     7	      i[0] = i[0].replace(/^--un-/, `--${prefix}`)
     8	      if (typeof i[1] === 'string')
     9	        i[1] = i[1].replace(/var\(--un-/g, `var(--${prefix}`)
    10	    })
    11	  }
    12	
    13	  return prefix !== 'un-' ? [processor] : []
    14	}
    15

    13	const bgLengthRE = /^\[(?:length|size):.+\]$/
    14	const bgPositionRE = /^\[position:.+\]$/
    15	const bgGradientRE = /^\[(?:linear|conic|radial)-gradient\(.+\)\]$/

    18	export const bgColors: Rule<Theme>[] = [
    19	  [/^bg-(.+)$/, (...args) => {
    20	    const d = args[0][1]
    21	    if (bgUrlRE.test(d))

    23	    if (bgLengthRE.test(d) && h.bracketOfLength(d) != null)

    25	    if ((isSize(d) || bgPositionRE.test(d)) && h.bracketOfPosition(d) != null)

    32	      }
    33	    }

     4	export function colorOpacityToString(color: CSSColorValue) {
     5	  const alpha = color.alpha ?? 1
     6	  return (typeof alpha === 'string' && alphaPlaceholders.includes(alpha))
     7	    ? 1

    10	
    11	export function colorToString(color: CSSColorValue | string, alphaOverride?: string | number) {
    12	  if (typeof color === 'string')
    13	    return color.replace(alphaPlaceholdersRE, `${alphaOverride ?? 1}`)
    14	
    15	  const { components } = color
    16	  let { alpha, type } = color
    17	  alpha = alphaOverride ?? alpha
    18	  type = type.toLowerCase()
    19	
    20	  if (['hsla', 'rgba'].includes(type))
    21	    return `${type}(${components.join(', ')}${alpha == null ? '' : `, ${alpha}`})`
    22	
    23	  alpha = alpha == null ? '' : ` / ${alpha}`
    24	  if (cssColorFunctions.includes(type))
    25	    return `${type}(${components.join(' ')}${alpha})`
    26	  return `color(${type} ${components.join(' ')}${alpha})`
    27	}

    11	// #region Number Resolver
    12	export function numberResolver(size: string, defaultValue?: string | number): number | undefined {
    13	  const v = h.number(size) ?? defaultValue
    14	
    15	  if (v != null) {
    16	    let num = Number(v)
    17	    if (String(v).endsWith('%')) {
    18	      num = Number(String(v).slice(0, -1)) / 100
    19	    }
    20	
    21	    return num
    22	  }
    23	}
    24	// #endregion
    25	
    26	// #region Direction with size
    27	/**
    28	 * Provide {@link DynamicMatcher} function returning spacing definition. See spacing rules.
    29	 *
    30	 * @param propertyPrefix - Property for the css value to be created. Postfix will be appended according to direction matched.
    31	 * @see {@link directionMap}
    32	 */
    33	export function directionSize(propertyPrefix: string): DynamicMatcher<Theme> {
    34	  function parseNumberWithUnit(str: string): [number | undefined, string | undefined] {
    35	    const match = str.match(numberWithUnitRE)
    36	    if (match) {
    37	      const [, n, unit] = match
    38	      const num = Number.parseFloat(n)
    39	      if (!Number.isNaN(num))
    40	        return [num, unit]
    41	    }
    42	    return [undefined, undefined]
    43	  }
    44	
    45	  function resolveSpace(theme: Theme) {
    46	    let base: number | undefined
    47	    let unit: string | undefined
    48	
    49	    if (theme.spacing?.DEFAULT) {
    50	      const [v, u] = parseNumberWithUnit(theme.spacing.DEFAULT)
    51	      if (v != null && u != null) {
    52	        base = v
    53	        unit = u
    54	      }
    55	    }
    56	
    57	    return Object.entries(theme.spacing ?? {}).reduce((acc, [key, value]) => {
    58	      const [v, u] = parseNumberWithUnit(value)
    59	
    60	      if (v != null && u != null && u === unit) {
    61	        acc[key] = v / base!
    62	      }
    63	      else {
    64	        acc[key] = value
    65	      }
    66	
    67	      return acc
    68	    }, {} as Record<string, number | string>)
    69	  }
    70	
    71	  return (([_, direction, size]: (string | undefined)[], { theme }): CSSEntries | undefined => {
    72	    if (size != null && direction != null) {
    73	      const spaceMap = resolveSpace(theme)
    74	      let v: string | number | undefined
    75	
    76	      const isNegative = size.startsWith('-')
    77	      if (isNegative)
    78	        size = size.slice(1)
    79	
    80	      v = numberResolver(size, spaceMap[size as keyof typeof spaceMap])
    81	
    82	      if (v != null) {
    83	        if (!Number.isNaN(v)) {
    84	          themeTracking('spacing')
    85	          return directionMap[direction].map(i => [`${propertyPrefix}${i}`, `calc(var(--spacing) * ${isNegative ? '-' : ''}${v})`])
    86	        }
    87	        else {
    88	          themeTracking('spacing', size)
    89	          return directionMap[direction].map(i => [`${propertyPrefix}${i}`, isNegative ? `calc(var(--spacing-${size} * -1)` : `var(--spacing-${size})`])
    90	        }
    91	      }
    92	
    93	      v = h.bracket.cssvar.global.auto.fraction.rem(isNegative ? `-${size}` : size)
    94	
    95	      if (v != null) {
    96	        return directionMap[direction].map(i => [`${propertyPrefix}${i}`, v])
    97	      }
    98	    }
    99	  }) as DynamicMatcher<Theme>
   100	}
   101	// #endregion
   102	
   103	// #region With Colors
   104	
   105	// #region Parse color
   106	
   107	/**
   108	 * Split utility shorthand delimited by / or :
   109	 */
   110	export function splitShorthand(body: string, type: string) {
   111	  const [front, rest] = getStringComponent(body, '[', ']', ['/', ':']) ?? []
   112	
   113	  if (front != null) {
   114	    const match = (front.match(bracketTypeRe) ?? [])[1]
   115	
   116	    if (match == null || match === type)
   117	      return [front, rest]
   118	  }
   119	}
   120	
   121	/**
   122	 * Parse color string into {@link ParsedColorValue} (if possible). Color value will first be matched to theme object before parsing.
   123	 * See also color.tests.ts for more examples.
   124	 *
   125	 * @example Parseable strings:
   126	 * 'red' // From theme, if 'red' is available
   127	 * 'red-100' // From theme, plus scale
   128	 * 'red-100/20' // From theme, plus scale/opacity
   129	 * '[rgb(100 2 3)]/[var(--op)]' // Bracket with rgb color and bracket with opacity
   130	 * '[rgb(100 2 3)]/[var(--op)]/[in_oklab]' // Bracket with rgb color, bracket with opacity and bracket with interpolation method
   131	 *
   132	 * @param body - Color string to be parsed.
   133	 * @param theme - {@link Theme} object.
   134	 * @return object if string is parseable.
   135	 */
   136	export function parseColor(body: string, theme: Theme) {
   137	  let split
   138	  const [front, ...rest] = getStringComponents(body, ['/', ':'], 3) ?? []
   139	
   140	  if (front != null) {
   141	    const match = (front.match(bracketTypeRe) ?? [])[1]
   142	
   143	    if (match == null || match === 'color') {
   144	      split = [front, ...rest]
   145	    }
   146	  }
   147	
   148	  if (!split)
   149	    return
   150	
   151	  let opacity: string | undefined
   152	  let [main, opacityOrModifier, modifier] = split as [string, string | undefined, string | undefined]
   153	
   154	  if (isInterpolatedMethod(opacityOrModifier) || isInterpolatedMethod(h.bracket(opacityOrModifier ?? ''))) {
   155	    modifier = opacityOrModifier
   156	  }
   157	  else {
   158	    opacity = opacityOrModifier
   159	  }
   160	
   161	  const colors = main
   162	    .replace(/([a-z])(\d)(?![-_a-z])/g, '$1-$2')
   163	    .split(/-/g)
   164	  const [name] = colors
   165	
   166	  if (!name)
   167	    return
   168	
   169	  let parsed = parseThemeColor(theme, colors)
   170	  if (!parsed && colors.length >= 2) {
   171	    // If the last part of the color is numbers, merge the last two parts
   172	    // e.g. ['foo', 'bar', '1'] should be parsed as ['foo', 'bar1']
   173	    // try the last key is `bar1` in the theme.
   174	    const last = colors.at(-1)
   175	    const secondLast = colors.at(-2)
   176	    if (/^\d+$/.test(last!)) {
   177	      const keys = colors.slice(0, -2).concat([`${secondLast}${last}`])
   178	      parsed = parseThemeColor(theme, keys)
   179	    }
   180	  }
   181	
   182	  let { no, keys, color } = parsed ?? {}
   183	
   184	  if (!color) {
   185	    const bracket = h.bracketOfColor(main)
   186	    const bracketOrMain = bracket || main
   187	
   188	    if (h.numberWithUnit(bracketOrMain))
   189	      return
   190	
   191	    if (/^#[\da-f]+$/i.test(bracketOrMain))
   192	      color = bracketOrMain
   193	    else if (/^hex-[\da-fA-F]+$/.test(bracketOrMain))
   194	      color = `#${bracketOrMain.slice(4)}`
   195	    else if (main.startsWith('$'))
   196	      color = h.cssvar(main)
   197	
   198	    color = color || bracket
   199	  }
   200	
   201	  return {
   202	    opacity,
   203	    modifier: (modifier && h.bracket.cssvar(modifier)) || modifier,
   204	    name,
   205	    no,
   206	    color: color ?? SpecialColorKey[name as keyof typeof SpecialColorKey],
   207	    alpha: h.bracket.cssvar.percent(opacity ?? ''),
   208	    /**
   209	     * Keys means the color is from theme object.
   210	     */
   211	    keys,
   212	    get cssColor() {
   213	      return parseCssColor(this.color)
   214	    },
   215	  }
   216	}
   217	
   218	export function parseThemeColor(theme: Theme, keys: string[]) {
   219	  let color: string | undefined
   220	  let no
   221	  let key
   222	
   223	  const colorData = getThemeByKey(theme, 'colors', keys)
   224	
   225	  if (typeof colorData === 'object') {
   226	    if ('DEFAULT' in colorData) {
   227	      color = colorData.DEFAULT
   228	      no = 'DEFAULT'
   229	      key = [...keys, no]
   230	    }
   231	  }
   232	  else if (typeof colorData === 'string') {
   233	    color = colorData
   234	    key = keys
   235	    no = keys.at(-1)
   236	  }
   237	
   238	  if (!color)
   239	    return
   240	
   241	  return {
   242	    color,
   243	    no,
   244	    keys: key,
   245	  }
   246	}
   247	
   248	export function getThemeByKey(theme: Theme, themeKey: keyof Theme, keys: string[]) {
   249	  const obj = theme[themeKey]
   250	  function deepGet(current: any, path: string[]): any {
   251	    if (!current || typeof current !== 'object')
   252	      return undefined
   253	    if (path.length === 0)
   254	      return current
   255	    // First, check if the path is a flat key (e.g., foo-bar)
   256	    for (let i = path.length; i > 0; i--) {
   257	      const flatKey = path.slice(0, i).join('-')
   258	      if (flatKey in current) {
   259	        const v = current[flatKey]
   260	        if (i === path.length)
   261	          return v
   262	        // look for the rest of the path
   263	        return deepGet(v, path.slice(i))
   264	      }
   265	    }
   266	    return undefined
   267	  }
   268	  return deepGet(obj, keys)
   269	}
   270	
   271	// #endregion
   272	
   273	// #region Color Resolver
   274	
   275	export function colorCSSGenerator(
   276	  data: ReturnType<typeof parseColor>,
   277	  property: string,
   278	  varName: string,
   279	  ctx?: RuleContext<Theme>,
   280	): [CSSObject, ...CSSValueInput[]] | undefined {
   281	  if (!data)
   282	    return
   283	
   284	  const { color, keys, alpha, modifier } = data
   285	  const rawColorComment = ctx?.generator.config.envMode === 'dev' && color ? ` /* ${color} */` : ''
   286	  const css: CSSObject = {}
   287	
   288	  if (color) {
   289	    const result: [CSSObject, ...CSSValueInput[]] = [css]
   290	
   291	    if (Object.values(SpecialColorKey).includes(color)) {
   292	      css[property] = color
   293	    }
   294	    else {
   295	      const alphaKey = `--un-${varName}-opacity`
   296	      const value = keys ? generateThemeVariable('colors', keys) : color
   297	      let method = modifier ?? (keys ? 'in srgb' : 'in oklab')
   298	      if (!method.startsWith('in ') && !method.startsWith('var(')) {
   299	        method = `in ${method}`
   300	      }
   301	
   302	      css[property] = `color-mix(${method}, ${value} ${alpha ?? `var(${alphaKey})`}, transparent)${rawColorComment}`
   303	      result.push(defineProperty(alphaKey, { syntax: '<percentage>', initialValue: '100%' }))
   304	
   305	      if (keys) {
   306	        themeTracking(`colors`, keys)
   307	        if (!modifier) {
   308	          result.push({
   309	            [symbols.parent]: '@supports (color: color-mix(in lab, red, red))',
   310	            [symbols.noMerge]: true,
   311	            [symbols.shortcutsNoMerge]: true,
   312	            [property]: `color-mix(in oklab, ${value} ${alpha ?? `var(${alphaKey})`}, transparent)${rawColorComment}`,
   313	          })
   314	        }
   315	      }
   316	      if (ctx?.theme) {
   317	        detectThemeValue(color, ctx.theme)
   318	      }
   319	    }
   320	
   321	    return result
   322	  }
   323	}
   324	
   325	export function colorResolver(property: string, varName: string) {
   326	  return ([, body]: string[], ctx: RuleContext<Theme>): (CSSValueInput | string)[] | undefined => {
   327	    const data = parseColor(body ?? '', ctx.theme)
   328	    if (!data)
   329	      return
   330	
   331	    return colorCSSGenerator(data, property, varName, ctx) as (CSSValueInput | string)[]
   332	  }
   333	}
   334	
   335	// #endregion
   336	
   337	export function colorableShadows(shadows: string | string[], colorVar: string) {
   338	  const colored = []
   339	  shadows = toArray(shadows)
   340	  for (let i = 0; i < shadows.length; i++) {
   341	    // shadow values are between 3 to 6 terms including color
   342	    const components = getStringComponents(shadows[i], ' ', 6)
   343	    if (!components || components.length < 3)
   344	      return shadows
   345	
   346	    let isInset = false
   347	    const pos = components.indexOf('inset')
   348	    if (pos !== -1) {
   349	      components.splice(pos, 1)
   350	      isInset = true
   351	    }
   352	
   353	    let colorVarValue = ''
   354	    const lastComp = components.at(-1)
   355	    if (parseCssColor(components.at(0))) {
   356	      const color = parseCssColor(components.shift())
   357	      if (color)
   358	        colorVarValue = `, ${colorToString(color)}`
   359	    }
   360	    else if (parseCssColor(lastComp)) {
   361	      const color = parseCssColor(components.pop())
   362	      if (color)
   363	        colorVarValue = `, ${colorToString(color)}`
   364	    }
   365	    else if (lastComp && cssVarFnRE.test(lastComp)) {
   366	      const color = components.pop()!
   367	      colorVarValue = `, ${color}`
   368	    }
   369	
   370	    colored.push(`${isInset ? 'inset ' : ''}${components.join(' ')} var(${colorVar}${colorVarValue})`)
   371	  }
   372	
   373	  return colored
   374	}
   375	
   376	export function hasParseableColor(color: string | undefined, theme: Theme) {
   377	  return color != null && !!parseColor(color, theme)?.color
   378	}
   379	
   380	// #endregion
   381	
   382	// #region resolve breakpoints
   383	const reLetters = /[a-z]+/gi
   384	const resolvedBreakpoints = new WeakMap<any, { point: string, size: string }[]>()
   385	
   386	export function resolveBreakpoints({ theme, generator }: Readonly<VariantContext<Theme>>, key: 'breakpoint' | 'verticalBreakpoint' = 'breakpoint') {
   387	  const breakpoints: Record<string, string> | undefined = (generator?.userConfig?.theme as any)?.[key] || theme[key]
   388	
   389	  if (!breakpoints)
   390	    return undefined
   391	
   392	  if (resolvedBreakpoints.has(theme))
   393	    return resolvedBreakpoints.get(theme)
   394	
   395	  const resolved = Object.entries(breakpoints)
   396	    .sort((a, b) => Number.parseInt(a[1].replace(reLetters, '')) - Number.parseInt(b[1].replace(reLetters, '')))
   397	    .map(([point, size]) => ({ point, size }))
   398	
   399	  resolvedBreakpoints.set(theme, resolved)
   400	  return resolved
   401	}
   402	
   403	export function resolveVerticalBreakpoints(context: Readonly<VariantContext<Theme>>) {
   404	  return resolveBreakpoints(context, 'verticalBreakpoint')
   405	}
   406	// #endregion
   407	
   408	// #region Global static & defineProperty
   409	export function makeGlobalStaticRules(prefix: string, property?: string): StaticRule[] {
   410	  return globalKeywords.map(keyword => [`${prefix}-${keyword}`, { [property ?? prefix]: keyword }])
   411	}
   412	
   413	export function defineProperty(
   414	  property: string,
   415	  options: { syntax?: string, inherits?: boolean, initialValue?: unknown } = {},
   416	): CSSValueInput {
   417	  const {
   418	    syntax = '*',
   419	    inherits = false,
   420	    initialValue,
   421	  } = options
   422	
   423	  const value: CSSObjectInput = {
   424	    [symbols.shortcutsNoMerge]: true,
   425	    [symbols.noMerge]: true,
   426	    [symbols.variants]: () => [
   427	      {
   428	        parent: '',
   429	        layer: 'properties',
   430	        selector: () => `@property ${property}`,
   431	      },
   432	    ],
   433	    syntax: JSON.stringify(syntax),
   434	    inherits: inherits ? 'true' : 'false',
   435	  }
   436	  if (initialValue != null) {
   437	    value['initial-value'] = initialValue as keyof CSSObjectInput
   438	  }
   439	  propertyTracking(property, initialValue ? String(initialValue) : 'initial')
   440	  return value
   441	}
   442	// #endregion
   443	
   444	// #region Basic util functions
   445	export function isCSSMathFn(value: string | undefined) {
   446	  return value != null && cssMathFnRE.test(value)
   447	}
   448	
   449	export function isSize(str: string) {
   450	  if (str[0] === '[' && str.slice(-1) === ']')
   451	    str = str.slice(1, -1)
   452	  return cssMathFnRE.test(str) || numberWithUnitRE.test(str)
   453	}
   454	
   455	export function camelize(str: string) {
   456	  return str.replace(/-(\w)/g, (_, c) => c ? c.toUpperCase() : '')
   457	}
   458	
   459	export function hyphenate(str: string) {
   460	  return str.replace(/(?:^|\B)([A-Z])/g, '-$1').toLowerCase()
   461	}
   462	
   463	export function compressCSS(css: string, isDev = false) {
   464	  if (isDev)
   465	    return css.trim()
   466	  return css.trim().replace(/\s+/g, ' ').replace(/\/\*[\s\S]*?\*\//g, '')
   467	}

Perfect! I can see the issue now. When `important` is set to a selector like `#__nuxt`, the postprocessor wraps all selectors with `#__nuxt :is(...)`, including the `@property` declarations, which is invalid CSS:

```css
#__nuxt :is(@property --un-text-opacity){...}
```

This should be:
```css
@property --un-text-opacity{...}
```

The `@property` at-rule should not be wrapped with the important selector. Let's look at the important postprocessor again:

     4	export function important({ important: option }: PresetWind4Options): Postprocessor[] {
     5	  if (option == null || option === false)
     6	    return []
     7	
     8	  const wrapWithIs = (selector: string) => {
     9	    if (selector.startsWith(':is(') && selector.endsWith(')'))
    10	      return selector
    11	
    12	    // handle pseudo
    13	    if (selector.includes('::'))
    14	      return selector.replace(/(.*?)((?:\s\*)?::.*)/, ':is($1)$2')
    15

    17	  }

    20	    option === true

    24	            return

I can see the issue now! When `option` is a string (like `#__nuxt`), the postprocessor on line 31-34 wraps the selector, but it doesn't check if the selector is an at-rule (like `@property`). The code on line 23-24 correctly handles the case when `option === true` by skipping the properties layer, but when `option` is a string selector, it should also skip the properties layer.

Let's check if there's any existing handling for at-rules or if we need to add it. Looking at line 32, it wraps all selectors starting with the option selector. The issue is that `@property` selectors should not be wrapped.

The fix is to add a check in the string case to skip the properties layer, similar to the `option === true` case. Let's update the code:

import presetWind4 from '"'"'@unocss/preset-wind4'"'"'

async function testWithPresetWind3() {
  console.log('"'"'\n=== Testing preset-wind3 with important selector ===\n'"'"')
  const presetWind3 = (await import('"'"'@unocss/preset-wind'"'"')).default
  
  const uno = await createGenerator({
    envMode: '"'"'dev'"'"',
    presets: [
      presetWind3({
        important: '"'"'#app'"'"',
      }),
    ],
  })

  const { css } = await uno.generate([
    '"'"'text-opacity-50'"'"',
    '"'"'text-red'"'"',
    '"'"'dark:bg-blue'"'"',
  ].join('"'"' '"'"'), { preflights: false })
  
  console.log('"'"'Generated CSS:'"'"')
  console.log(css)
  console.log('"'"'\n'"'"')
}

async function testWithPresetWind4() {
  console.log('"'"'\n=== Testing preset-wind4 with important selector ===\n'"'"')
  
  const uno = await createGenerator({
    envMode: '"'"'dev'"'"',
    presets: [
      presetWind4({
        important: '"'"'#__nuxt'"'"',
        preflights: { reset: false },
      }),
    ],
  })

  const { css } = await uno.generate([
    '"'"'text-opacity-50'"'"',
    '"'"'text-red'"'"',
    '"'"'dark:bg-blue'"'"',
  ].join('"'"' '"'"'), { preflights: false })
  
  console.log('"'"'Generated CSS:'"'"')
  console.log(css)
  
  // Check if @property is not wrapped
  const hasInvalidProperty = css.includes('"'"'#__nuxt :is(@property'"'"')
  const hasValidProperty = css.includes('"'"'@property --un-text-opacity'"'"') && !css.includes('"'"'#__nuxt :is(@property'"'"')
  
  console.log('"'"'\n--- Validation ---'"'"')
  console.log('"'"'Has invalid @property wrapping:'"'"', hasInvalidProperty)
  console.log('"'"'Has valid @property declaration:'"'"', hasValidProperty)
  console.log('"'"'Test passed:'"'"', !hasInvalidProperty && hasValidProperty)
  console.log('"'"'\n'"'"')
}

async function testEdgeCases() {
  console.log('"'"'\n=== Testing edge cases ===\n'"'"')
  
  const uno = await createGenerator({
    envMode: '"'"'dev'"'"',
    presets: [
      presetWind4({
        important: '"'"'#app'"'"',
        preflights: { reset: false },
      }),
    ],
  })

  // Test various utilities that use CSS variables
  const utilities = [
    '"'"'text-red'"'"',
    '"'"'bg-blue'"'"',
    '"'"'text-opacity-50'"'"',
    '"'"'bg-opacity-75'"'"',
    '"'"'border-green'"'"',
    '"'"'ring-red'"'"',
    '"'"'text-shadow-red'"'"',
  ]
  
  const { css } = await uno.generate(utilities.join('"'"' '"'"'), { preflights: false })
  
  console.log('"'"'Generated CSS for multiple utilities:'"'"')
  console.log(css)
  
  // Check that all @property declarations are valid
  const propertyMatches = css.match(/@property[^{]+/g) || []
  const invalidProperties = propertyMatches.filter(prop => prop.includes('"'"'#app :is('"'"'))
  
  console.log('"'"'\n--- Validation ---'"'"')
  console.log('"'"'Total @property declarations:'"'"', propertyMatches.length)
  console.log('"'"'Invalid @property declarations:'"'"', invalidProperties.length)
  if (invalidProperties.length > 0) {
    console.log('"'"'Invalid declarations:'"'"')
    invalidProperties.forEach(prop => console.log('"'"'  -'"'"', prop))
  }
  console.log('"'"'Test passed:'"'"', invalidProperties.length === 0)
  console.log('"'"'\n'"'"')
}

async function testImportantTrue() {
  console.log('"'"'\n=== Testing important: true ===\n'"'"')
  
  const uno = await createGenerator({
    envMode: '"'"'dev'"'"',
    presets: [
      presetWind4({
        important: true,
        preflights: { reset: false },
      }),
    ],
  })

  const { css } = await uno.generate('"'"'text-red text-opacity-50'"'"', { preflights: false })
  
  console.log('"'"'Generated CSS:'"'"')
  console.log(css)
  
  // Check that properties layer doesn'"'"'t have !important
  const lines = css.split('"'"'\n'"'"')
  const propertiesLayer = lines.slice(
    lines.findIndex(l => l.includes('"'"'/* layer: properties */'"'"')),
    lines.findIndex((l, i) => i > 0 && l.includes('"'"'/* layer:'"'"'))
  ).join('"'"'\n'"'"')
  
  const hasImportantInProperties = propertiesLayer.includes('"'"'!important'"'"')
  
  console.log('"'"'\n--- Validation ---'"'"')
  console.log('"'"'Has !important in properties layer:'"'"', hasImportantInProperties)
  console.log('"'"'Test passed:'"'"', !hasImportantInProperties)
  console.log('"'"'\n'"'"')
}

  }
  
  await testWithPresetWind4()
  await testEdgeCases()
  await testImportantTrue()
}

async function testPlaygroundExample() {
  console.log('"'"'\n=== Testing playground example from issue ===\n'"'"')
  
  const uno = await createGenerator({
    envMode: '"'"'dev'"'"',
    presets: [
      presetWind4({
        important: '"'"'#__nuxt'"'"',
      }),
    ],
  })

  // Based on the issue report, the problem occurs with any font color
  const { css } = await uno.generate('"'"'text-red'"'"', { preflights: true })
  
  console.log('"'"'Generated CSS:'"'"')
  console.log(css)
  console.log('"'"'\n'"'"')
  
  // Validate the fix
  console.log('"'"'--- Validation ---'"'"')
  
  // Check that @property is properly defined and not wrapped
  const hasInvalidPropertyWrapping = css.includes('"'"'#__nuxt :is(@property'"'"')
  const hasValidPropertyDeclaration = css.includes('"'"'@property --un-text-opacity'"'"')
  
  // Check that the CSS variable is properly defined
  const hasPropertyDefinition = css.match(/@property --un-text-opacity\{[^}]*syntax:"<percentage>"/)
  
  // Check that color uses the CSS variable
  const usesTextOpacityVar = css.includes('"'"'var(--un-text-opacity)'"'"')
  
  console.log('"'"'✗ Has invalid @property wrapping:'"'"', hasInvalidPropertyWrapping)
  console.log('"'"'✓ Has valid @property declaration:'"'"', hasValidPropertyDeclaration)
  console.log('"'"'✓ Has proper @property definition:'"'"', !!hasPropertyDefinition)
  console.log('"'"'✓ Uses --un-text-opacity variable:'"'"', usesTextOpacityVar)
  console.log('"'"'\n'"'"')
  
  if (!hasInvalidPropertyWrapping && hasValidPropertyDeclaration && hasPropertyDefinition && usesTextOpacityVar) {
    console.log('"'"'✅ ISSUE FIXED: All validations passed!'"'"')
    console.log('"'"'   - @property declarations are not wrapped with the important selector'"'"')
    console.log('"'"'   - --un-text-opacity CSS variable is properly defined'"'"')
    console.log('"'"'   - Color styles correctly reference the CSS variable'"'"')
  } else {
    console.log('"'"'❌ ISSUE NOT FIXED: Some validations failed!'"'"')
  }
  console.log('"'"'\n'"'"')
}

async function testVariousImportantSelectors() {
  console.log('"'"'\n=== Testing various important selectors ===\n'"'"')
  
  const selectors = ['"'"'#app'"'"', '"'"'#__nuxt'"'"', '"'"'.main-wrapper'"'"', '"'"'#root'"'"']
  
  for (const selector of selectors) {
    console.log(`Testing with important: "${selector}"`)
    
    const uno = await createGenerator({
      envMode: '"'"'dev'"'"',
      presets: [
        presetWind4({
          important: selector,
          preflights: { reset: false },
        }),
      ],
    })

    const { css } = await uno.generate('"'"'text-red bg-blue border-green'"'"', { preflights: false })
    
    // Check that @property declarations are not wrapped
    const hasInvalidPropertyWrapping = css.includes(`${selector} :is(@property`)
    const propertyDeclarations = css.match(/@property --un-[a-z-]+/g) || []
    
    if (hasInvalidPropertyWrapping) {
      console.log(`  ❌ FAIL: @property declarations are wrapped with "${selector}"`)
    } else if (propertyDeclarations.length > 0) {
      console.log(`  ✓ PASS: ${propertyDeclarations.length} @property declarations are not wrapped`)
    } else {
      console.log(`  ⚠ WARNING: No @property declarations found`)
    }
    
    // Check that regular selectors are wrapped
    const hasWrappedSelectors = css.includes(`${selector} :is(.text-red)`)
    if (hasWrappedSelectors) {
      console.log(`  ✓ PASS: Regular selectors are properly wrapped`)
    } else {
      console.log(`  ❌ FAIL: Regular selectors are not wrapped`)
    }
    console.log('"'"''"'"')
  }
}

async function testPropertiesLayerWithVariousUtilities() {
  console.log('"'"'\n=== Testing properties layer with various utilities ===\n'"'"')
  
  const uno = await createGenerator({
    envMode: '"'"'dev'"'"',
    presets: [
      presetWind4({
        important: '"'"'#app'"'"',
        preflights: { reset: false },
      }),
    ],
  })

  const utilities = [
    // Color utilities
    '"'"'text-red'"'"', '"'"'text-opacity-50'"'"',
    '"'"'bg-blue'"'"', '"'"'bg-opacity-75'"'"',
    '"'"'border-green'"'"', '"'"'border-opacity-25'"'"',
    // Shadow utilities
    '"'"'text-shadow-red'"'"',
    '"'"'shadow-red'"'"',
    // Ring utilities
    '"'"'ring-red'"'"', '"'"'ring-opacity-50'"'"',
    // Decoration utilities
    '"'"'decoration-red'"'"',
  ]

  const { css } = await uno.generate(utilities.join('"'"' '"'"'), { preflights: false })
  
  // Extract all @property declarations
  const propertyMatches = css.match(/@property[^{]+\{[^}]+\}/g) || []
  
  console.log(`Total @property declarations: ${propertyMatches.length}`)
  
  // Check that none of them are wrapped with the important selector
  const invalidProperties = propertyMatches.filter(prop => prop.includes('"'"'#app :is('"'"'))
  
  if (invalidProperties.length > 0) {
    console.log(`❌ FAIL: ${invalidProperties.length} properties are incorrectly wrapped`)
    invalidProperties.forEach(prop => {
      console.log(`  - ${prop.substring(0, 60)}...`)
    })
  } else {
    console.log('"'"'✓ PASS: All @property declarations are valid'"'"')
  }
  
  // Check that all properties have proper syntax
  const propertiesWithSyntax = propertyMatches.filter(prop => prop.includes('"'"'syntax:'"'"'))
  console.log(`Properties with syntax: ${propertiesWithSyntax.length}/${propertyMatches.length}`)
  
  if (propertiesWithSyntax.length === propertyMatches.length) {
    console.log('"'"'✓ PASS: All @property declarations have proper syntax definition'"'"')
  } else {
    console.log('"'"'❌ FAIL: Some @property declarations are missing syntax'"'"')
  }
  
  console.log('"'"''"'"')
}

async function testBothImportantModes() {
  console.log('"'"'\n=== Testing both important modes (true vs selector) ===\n'"'"')
  
  // Test with important: true
  const unoTrue = await createGenerator({
    envMode: '"'"'dev'"'"',
    presets: [
      presetWind4({
        important: true,
        preflights: { reset: false },
      }),
    ],
  })

  const { css: cssTrue } = await unoTrue.generate('"'"'text-red text-opacity-50'"'"', { preflights: false })
  
  console.log('"'"'Testing important: true'"'"')
  
  // Check that @property doesn'"'"'t have !important
  const propertiesSection = cssTrue.split('"'"'/* layer: properties */'"'"')[1]?.split('"'"'/* layer:'"'"')[0] || '"'"''"'"'
  const hasImportantInProperties = propertiesSection.includes('"'"'!important'"'"')
  
  if (hasImportantInProperties) {
    console.log('"'"'  ❌ FAIL: @property declarations have !important'"'"')
  } else {
    console.log('"'"'  ✓ PASS: @property declarations do not have !important'"'"')
  }
  
  // Check that regular CSS has !important
  const defaultSection = cssTrue.split('"'"'/* layer: default */'"'"')[1] || '"'"''"'"'
  const hasImportantInDefault = defaultSection.includes('"'"'!important'"'"')
  
  if (hasImportantInDefault) {
    console.log('"'"'  ✓ PASS: Default layer has !important'"'"')
  } else {
    console.log('"'"'  ❌ FAIL: Default layer does not have !important'"'"')
  }
  
  // Test with important: '"'"'#app'"'"'
  const unoSelector = await createGenerator({
    envMode: '"'"'dev'"'"',
    presets: [
      presetWind4({
        important: '"'"'#app'"'"',
        preflights: { reset: false },
      }),
    ],
  })

  const { css: cssSelector } = await unoSelector.generate('"'"'text-red text-opacity-50'"'"', { preflights: false })
  
  console.log('"'"'\nTesting important: "#app"'"'"')
  
  // Check that @property is not wrapped
  const hasInvalidPropertyWrapping = cssSelector.includes('"'"'#app :is(@property'"'"')
  
  if (hasInvalidPropertyWrapping) {
    console.log('"'"'  ❌ FAIL: @property declarations are wrapped with selector'"'"')
  } else {
    console.log('"'"'  ✓ PASS: @property declarations are not wrapped'"'"')
  }
  
  // Check that regular selectors are wrapped
  const hasWrappedSelectors = cssSelector.includes('"'"'#app :is(.text-red)'"'"')
  
  if (hasWrappedSelectors) {
    console.log('"'"'  ✓ PASS: Regular selectors are wrapped with important selector'"'"')
  } else {
    console.log('"'"'  ❌ FAIL: Regular selectors are not wrapped'"'"')
  }
  
  console.log('"'"''"'"')
}

  await testVariousImportantSelectors()
  await testPropertiesLayerWithVariousUtilities()
  await testBothImportantModes()
  
  console.log('"'"'\n=== All tests completed ===\n'"'"')
}

import presetWind4 from '"'"'@unocss/preset-wind4'"'"'

async function testImportantWithVarPrefix() {
  console.log('"'"'\n=== Testing important with custom variablePrefix ===\n'"'"')
  
  const uno = await createGenerator({
    envMode: '"'"'dev'"'"',
    presets: [
      presetWind4({
        important: '"'"'#app'"'"',
        variablePrefix: '"'"'my-'"'"',
        preflights: { reset: false },
      }),
    ],
  })

  const { css } = await uno.generate('"'"'text-red text-opacity-50'"'"', { preflights: false })
  
  console.log('"'"'Generated CSS:'"'"')
  console.log(css)
  console.log('"'"'\n'"'"')
  
  console.log('"'"'--- Validation ---'"'"')
  
  // Check that @property uses custom prefix
  const hasCustomPrefixProperty = css.includes('"'"'@property --my-text-opacity'"'"')
  console.log('"'"'✓ Has @property with custom prefix (--my-text-opacity):'"'"', hasCustomPrefixProperty)
  
  // Check that @property is not wrapped
  const hasInvalidWrapping = css.includes('"'"'#app :is(@property'"'"')
  console.log('"'"'✓ @property not wrapped with important selector:'"'"', !hasInvalidWrapping)
  
  // Check that CSS uses custom prefix in var()
  const usesCustomPrefix = css.includes('"'"'var(--my-text-opacity)'"'"')
  console.log('"'"'✓ CSS uses custom prefix in var():'"'"', usesCustomPrefix)
  
  // Check that regular selectors are wrapped
  const hasWrappedSelectors = css.includes('"'"'#app :is(.text-red)'"'"')
  console.log('"'"'✓ Regular selectors are wrapped:'"'"', hasWrappedSelectors)
  
  if (hasCustomPrefixProperty && !hasInvalidWrapping && usesCustomPrefix && hasWrappedSelectors) {
    console.log('"'"'\n✅ All validations passed!'"'"')
  } else {
    console.log('"'"'\n❌ Some validations failed!'"'"')
  }
}

async function testImportantWithPrefix() {
  console.log('"'"'\n=== Testing important with utility prefix ===\n'"'"')
  
  const uno = await createGenerator({
    envMode: '"'"'dev'"'"',
    presets: [
      presetWind4({
        important: '"'"'#app'"'"',
        prefix: '"'"'tw-'"'"',
        preflights: { reset: false },
      }),
    ],
  })

  const { css } = await uno.generate('"'"'tw-text-red tw-text-opacity-50'"'"', { preflights: false })
  
  console.log('"'"'Generated CSS (excerpt):'"'"')
  const lines = css.split('"'"'\n'"'"').slice(0, 10)
  lines.forEach(line => console.log(line))
  console.log('"'"'...\n'"'"')
  
  console.log('"'"'--- Validation ---'"'"')
  
  // Check that @property is not wrapped
  const hasInvalidWrapping = css.includes('"'"'#app :is(@property'"'"')
  console.log('"'"'✓ @property not wrapped with important selector:'"'"', !hasInvalidWrapping)
  
  // Check that regular selectors use prefix
  const hasWrappedPrefixedSelectors = css.includes('"'"'#app :is(.tw-text-red)'"'"')
  console.log('"'"'✓ Prefixed selectors are wrapped:'"'"', hasWrappedPrefixedSelectors)
  
  if (!hasInvalidWrapping && hasWrappedPrefixedSelectors) {
    console.log('"'"'\n✅ All validations passed!'"'"')
  } else {
    console.log('"'"'\n❌ Some validations failed!'"'"')
  }
}

async function testMultipleOptions() {
  console.log('"'"'\n=== Testing with multiple options combined ===\n'"'"')
  
  const uno = await createGenerator({
    envMode: '"'"'dev'"'"',
    presets: [
      presetWind4({
        important: '"'"'#__nuxt'"'"',
        variablePrefix: '"'"'uno-'"'"',
        prefix: '"'"'u-'"'"',
        preflights: { reset: false },
      }),
    ],
  })

  const { css } = await uno.generate('"'"'u-text-red u-bg-blue'"'"', { preflights: false })
  
  console.log('"'"'--- Validation ---'"'"')
  
  // Check that @property uses custom variable prefix
  const hasCustomVarPrefix = css.includes('"'"'@property --uno-text-opacity'"'"')
  console.log('"'"'✓ @property uses custom variable prefix (--uno-):'"'"', hasCustomVarPrefix)
  
  // Check that @property is not wrapped
  const hasInvalidWrapping = css.includes('"'"'#__nuxt :is(@property'"'"')
  console.log('"'"'✓ @property not wrapped with important selector:'"'"', !hasInvalidWrapping)
  
  // Check that CSS uses custom variable prefix
  const usesCustomVarPrefix = css.includes('"'"'var(--uno-text-opacity)'"'"')
  console.log('"'"'✓ CSS uses custom variable prefix:'"'"', usesCustomVarPrefix)
  
  // Check that regular selectors use utility prefix and are wrapped
  const hasWrappedPrefixedSelectors = css.includes('"'"'#__nuxt :is(.u-text-red)'"'"')
  console.log('"'"'✓ Prefixed selectors are wrapped with important:'"'"', hasWrappedPrefixedSelectors)
  
  if (hasCustomVarPrefix && !hasInvalidWrapping && usesCustomVarPrefix && hasWrappedPrefixedSelectors) {
    console.log('"'"'\n✅ All validations passed!'"'"')
  } else {
    console.log('"'"'\n❌ Some validations failed!'"'"')
  }
}

async function runAllTests() {
  await testImportantWithVarPrefix()
  await testImportantWithPrefix()
  await testMultipleOptions()
  
  console.log('"'"'\n=== All combination tests completed ===\n'"'"')
}

runAllTests()

     1	import type { Postprocessor } from '@unocss/core'
     2	import type { PresetWind4Options } from '..'
     3	
     4	export function varPrefix({ variablePrefix: prefix }: PresetWind4Options): Postprocessor[] {
     5	  const processor: Postprocessor = (obj) => {
     6	    obj.entries.forEach((i) => {
     7	      i[0] = i[0].replace(/^--un-/, `--${prefix}`)
     8	      if (typeof i[1] === 'string')
     9	        i[1] = i[1].replace(/var\(--un-/g, `var(--${prefix}`)
    10	    })
    11	  }
    12	
    13	  return prefix !== 'un-' ? [processor] : []
    14	}

async function testPropertyStructure() {
  const uno = await createGenerator({

     1	import type { Postprocessor } from '@unocss/core'
     2	import type { PresetWind4Options } from '..'
     3	
     4	export function varPrefix({ variablePrefix: prefix }: PresetWind4Options): Postprocessor[] {
     5	  const processor: Postprocessor = (obj) => {
     6	    obj.entries.forEach((i) => {
     7	      i[0] = i[0].replace(/^--un-/, `--${prefix}`)
     8	      if (typeof i[1] === 'string')
     9	        i[1] = i[1].replace(/var\(--un-/g, `var(--${prefix}`)
    10	    })
    11	  }
    12	
    13	  return prefix !== 'un-' ? [processor] : []
    14	}

import { createGenerator } from '@unocss/core'
import presetWind4 from '@unocss/preset-wind4'

console.log('\n=== Final Comprehensive Validation ===\n')

async function validate() {
  // Test 1: Basic important with selector
  console.log('Test 1: Basic important with selector (#__nuxt)')
  const uno1 = await createGenerator({
    envMode: 'dev',
    presets: [
      presetWind4({
        important: '#__nuxt',
        preflights: { reset: false },
      }),
    ],
  })
  const { css: css1 } = await uno1.generate('text-red', { preflights: false })
  const test1Pass = 
    css1.includes('@property --un-text-opacity') &&
    !css1.includes('#__nuxt :is(@property') &&
    css1.includes('#__nuxt :is(.text-red)')
  console.log(test1Pass ? '✅ PASS' : '❌ FAIL')
  
  // Test 2: Important with selector + variablePrefix
  console.log('\nTest 2: Important with selector + variablePrefix')
  const uno2 = await createGenerator({
    envMode: 'dev',
    presets: [
      presetWind4({
        important: '#app',
        variablePrefix: 'my-',
        preflights: { reset: false },
      }),
    ],
  })
  const { css: css2 } = await uno2.generate('text-red', { preflights: false })
  const test2Pass = 
    css2.includes('@property --my-text-opacity') &&
    !css2.includes('#app :is(@property') &&
    css2.includes('var(--my-text-opacity)') &&
    css2.includes('#app :is(.text-red)')
  console.log(test2Pass ? '✅ PASS' : '❌ FAIL')
  
  // Test 3: Important with selector + prefix
  console.log('\nTest 3: Important with selector + utility prefix')
  const uno3 = await createGenerator({
    envMode: 'dev',
    presets: [
      presetWind4({
        important: '#app',
        prefix: 'tw-',
        preflights: { reset: false },
      }),
    ],
  })
  const { css: css3 } = await uno3.generate('tw-text-red', { preflights: false })
  const test3Pass = 
    css3.includes('@property --un-text-opacity') &&
    !css3.includes('#app :is(@property') &&
    css3.includes('#app :is(.tw-text-red)')
  console.log(test3Pass ? '✅ PASS' : '❌ FAIL')
  
  // Test 4: All options combined
  console.log('\nTest 4: All options combined')
  const uno4 = await createGenerator({
    envMode: 'dev',
    presets: [
      presetWind4({
        important: '#__nuxt',
        variablePrefix: 'uno-',
        prefix: 'u-',
        preflights: { reset: false },
      }),
    ],
  })
  const { css: css4 } = await uno4.generate('u-text-red', { preflights: false })
  const test4Pass = 
    css4.includes('@property --uno-text-opacity') &&
    !css4.includes('#__nuxt :is(@property') &&
    css4.includes('var(--uno-text-opacity)') &&
    css4.includes('#__nuxt :is(.u-text-red)')
  console.log(test4Pass ? '✅ PASS' : '❌ FAIL')
  
  // Test 5: Important true (should not wrap @property)
  console.log('\nTest 5: Important true')
  const uno5 = await createGenerator({
    envMode: 'dev',
    presets: [
      presetWind4({
        important: true,
        preflights: { reset: false },
      }),
    ],
  })
  const { css: css5 } = await uno5.generate('text-red', { preflights: false })
  const propertiesSection = css5.split('/* layer: properties */')[1]?.split('/* layer:')[0] || ''
  const test5Pass = 
    css5.includes('@property --un-text-opacity') &&
    !propertiesSection.includes('!important') &&
    css5.includes('!important') // Should be in default layer
  console.log(test5Pass ? '✅ PASS' : '❌ FAIL')
  
  // Test 6: Multiple color utilities
  console.log('\nTest 6: Multiple color utilities with important selector')
  const uno6 = await createGenerator({
    envMode: 'dev',
    presets: [
      presetWind4({
        important: '#app',
        preflights: { reset: false },
      }),
    ],
  })
  const { css: css6 } = await uno6.generate('text-red bg-blue border-green ring-yellow', { preflights: false })
  const propertyCount = (css6.match(/@property --un-[a-z-]+/g) || []).length
  const invalidWrappings = (css6.match(/#app :is\(@property/g) || []).length
  const test6Pass = propertyCount > 0 && invalidWrappings === 0
  console.log(test6Pass ? `✅ PASS (${propertyCount} properties, 0 invalid wrappings)` : '❌ FAIL')
  
  console.log('\n' + '='.repeat(50))
  const allPass = test1Pass && test2Pass && test3Pass && test4Pass && test5Pass && test6Pass
  if (allPass) {
    console.log('✅ ALL TESTS PASSED!')
    console.log('The issue is completely fixed:')
    console.log('  - @property declarations are never wrapped with important selector')
    console.log('  - @property declarations never have !important')
    console.log('  - @property declarations properly handle custom variable prefixes')
    console.log('  - Regular selectors are correctly wrapped when using important selector')
    console.log('  - Regular CSS properties correctly have !important when using important: true')
  } else {
    console.log('❌ SOME TESTS FAILED')
  }
  console.log('='.repeat(50) + '\n')
}

cd /testbed && cat > test_final_fixed.ts << 'EOF'
import { createGenerator } from '@unocss/core'
import presetWind4 from '@unocss/preset-wind4'

console.log('\n=== Final Comprehensive Validation ===\n')

async function validate() {
  // Test 1: Basic important with selector
  console.log('Test 1: Basic important with selector (#__nuxt)')
  const uno1 = await createGenerator({
    envMode: 'dev',
    presets: [
      presetWind4({
        important: '#__nuxt',
        preflights: { reset: false },
      }),
    ],
  })
  const { css: css1 } = await uno1.generate('text-red', { preflights: false })
  const test1Pass = 
    css1.includes('@property --un-text-opacity') &&
    !css1.includes('#__nuxt :is(@property') &&
    css1.includes('#__nuxt :is(.text-red)')
  console.log(test1Pass ? '✅ PASS' : '❌ FAIL')
  
  // Test 2: Important with selector + variablePrefix
  console.log('\nTest 2: Important with selector + variablePrefix')
  const uno2 = await createGenerator({
    envMode: 'dev',
    presets: [
      presetWind4({
        important: '#app',
        variablePrefix: 'my-',
        preflights: { reset: false },
      }),
    ],
  })
  const { css: css2 } = await uno2.generate('text-red', { preflights: false })
  const test2Pass = 
    css2.includes('@property --my-text-opacity') &&
    !css2.includes('#app :is(@property') &&
    css2.includes('var(--my-text-opacity)') &&
    css2.includes('#app :is(.text-red)')
  console.log(test2Pass ? '✅ PASS' : '❌ FAIL')
  
  // Test 3: Important with selector + prefix
  console.log('\nTest 3: Important with selector + utility prefix')
  const uno3 = await createGenerator({
    envMode: 'dev',
    presets: [
      presetWind4({
        important: '#app',
        prefix: 'tw-',
        preflights: { reset: false },
      }),
    ],
  })
  const { css: css3 } = await uno3.generate('tw-text-red', { preflights: false })
  const test3Pass = 
    css3.includes('@property --un-text-opacity') &&
    !css3.includes('#app :is(@property') &&
    css3.includes('#app :is(.tw-text-red)')
  console.log(test3Pass ? '✅ PASS' : '❌ FAIL')
  
  // Test 4: All options combined
  console.log('\nTest 4: All options combined')
  const uno4 = await createGenerator({
    envMode: 'dev',
    presets: [
      presetWind4({
        important: '#__nuxt',
        variablePrefix: 'uno-',
        prefix: 'u-',
        preflights: { reset: false },
      }),
    ],
  })
  const { css: css4 } = await uno4.generate('u-text-red', { preflights: false })
  const test4Pass = 
    css4.includes('@property --uno-text-opacity') &&
    !css4.includes('#__nuxt :is(@property') &&
    css4.includes('var(--uno-text-opacity)') &&
    css4.includes('#__nuxt :is(.u-text-red)')
  console.log(test4Pass ? '✅ PASS' : '❌ FAIL')
  
  // Test 5: Important true (should not add !important to @property)
  console.log('\nTest 5: Important true')
  const uno5 = await createGenerator({
    envMode: 'dev',
    presets: [
      presetWind4({
        important: true,
        preflights: { reset: false },
      }),
    ],
  })
  const { css: css5 } = await uno5.generate('text-red', { preflights: false })
  // Check that @property declaration doesn't have !important
  const propertyDecl = css5.match(/@property[^}]+}/)?.[0] || ''
  const propertyHasImportant = propertyDecl.includes('!important')
  // Check that the color CSS has !important
  const colorHasImportant = css5.includes('color:') && css5.includes('!important')
  const test5Pass = 
    css5.includes('@property --un-text-opacity') &&
    !propertyHasImportant &&
    colorHasImportant
  console.log(test5Pass ? '✅ PASS' : '❌ FAIL')
  if (!test5Pass) {
    console.log('  Property has !important:', propertyHasImportant)
    console.log('  Color has !important:', colorHasImportant)
  }
  
  // Test 6: Multiple color utilities
  console.log('\nTest 6: Multiple color utilities with important selector')
  const uno6 = await createGenerator({
    envMode: 'dev',
    presets: [
      presetWind4({
        important: '#app',
        preflights: { reset: false },
      }),
    ],
  })
  const { css: css6 } = await uno6.generate('text-red bg-blue border-green ring-yellow', { preflights: false })
  const propertyMatches = css6.match(/@property --un-[a-z-]+/g) || []
  const invalidWrappings = css6.includes('#app :is(@property')
  const test6Pass = propertyMatches.length > 0 && !invalidWrappings
  console.log(test6Pass ? `✅ PASS (${propertyMatches.length} properties, no invalid wrappings)` : '❌ FAIL')
  if (!test6Pass) {
    console.log('  Properties found:', propertyMatches.length)
    console.log('  Invalid wrappings:', invalidWrappings)
  }
  
  console.log('\n' + '='.repeat(50))
  const allPass = test1Pass && test2Pass && test3Pass && test4Pass && test5Pass && test6Pass
  if (allPass) {
    console.log('✅ ALL TESTS PASSED!')
    console.log('\nThe issue is completely fixed:')
    console.log('  ✓ @property declarations are never wrapped with important selector')
    console.log('  ✓ @property declarations never have !important')
    console.log('  ✓ @property declarations properly handle custom variable prefixes')
    console.log('  ✓ Regular selectors are correctly wrapped when using important selector')
    console.log('  ✓ Regular CSS properties correctly have !important when using important: true')
  } else {
    console.log('❌ SOME TESTS FAILED')
  }
  console.log('='.repeat(50) + '\n')
}

validate()

import { createGenerator } from '@unocss/core'
import presetWind4 from '@unocss/preset-wind4'

console.log('\n' + '='.repeat(60))
console.log('FINAL COMPREHENSIVE VALIDATION')
console.log('Testing the fix for: presetWind4 important selector wrapping @property')
console.log('='.repeat(60) + '\n')

async function runTests() {
  let passCount = 0
  let failCount = 0
  
  // Test 1: Original issue reproduction
  console.log('Test 1: Original Issue - important: "#__nuxt" with text-red')
  try {
    const uno = await createGenerator({
      envMode: 'dev',
      presets: [
        presetWind4({
          important: '#__nuxt',
        }),
      ],
    })
    const { css } = await uno.generate('text-red', { preflights: true })
    
    const hasProperty = css.includes('@property --un-text-opacity')
    const notWrapped = !css.includes('#__nuxt :is(@property')
    const usesVar = css.includes('var(--un-text-opacity)')
    const selectorWrapped = css.includes('#__nuxt :is(.text-red)')
    
    if (hasProperty && notWrapped && usesVar && selectorWrapped) {
      console.log('  ✅ PASS - Issue is fixed!')
      passCount++
    } else {
      console.log('  ❌ FAIL')
      console.log('    - Has @property:', hasProperty)
      console.log('    - Not wrapped:', notWrapped)
      console.log('    - Uses var:', usesVar)
      console.log('    - Selector wrapped:', selectorWrapped)
      failCount++
    }
  } catch (e) {
    console.log('  ❌ ERROR:', e.message)
    failCount++
  }
  
  // Test 2: Multiple important selectors
  console.log('\nTest 2: Various important selectors (#app, #root, .wrapper)')
  try {
    for (const selector of ['#app', '#root', '.wrapper']) {
      const uno = await createGenerator({
        envMode: 'dev',
        presets: [
          presetWind4({
            important: selector,
            preflights: { reset: false },
          }),
        ],
      })
      const { css } = await uno.generate('text-red', { preflights: false })
      
      const notWrapped = !css.includes(`${selector} :is(@property`)
      const selectorWrapped = css.includes(`${selector} :is(.text-red)`)
      
      if (!notWrapped || !selectorWrapped) {
        console.log(`  ❌ FAIL for selector "${selector}"`)
        failCount++
        return
      }
    }
    console.log('  ✅ PASS - All selectors work correctly')
    passCount++
  } catch (e) {
    console.log('  ❌ ERROR:', e.message)
    failCount++
  }
  
  // Test 3: important: true
  console.log('\nTest 3: important: true (should use !important, not wrap)')
  try {
    const uno = await createGenerator({
      envMode: 'dev',
      presets: [
        presetWind4({
          important: true,
          preflights: { reset: false },
        }),
      ],
    })
    const { css } = await uno.generate('text-red', { preflights: false })
    
    const hasProperty = css.includes('@property --un-text-opacity')
    const propertyMatch = css.match(/@property[^}]+}/)?.[0] || ''
    const propertyNoImportant = !propertyMatch.includes('!important')
    const colorHasImportant = css.includes('color:') && css.includes('!important')
    
    if (hasProperty && propertyNoImportant && colorHasImportant) {
      console.log('  ✅ PASS - @property not affected, colors have !important')
      passCount++
    } else {
      console.log('  ❌ FAIL')
      console.log('    - Has @property:', hasProperty)
      console.log('    - @property no !important:', propertyNoImportant)
      console.log('    - Color has !important:', colorHasImportant)
      failCount++
    }
  } catch (e) {
    console.log('  ❌ ERROR:', e.message)
    failCount++
  }
  
  // Test 4: Custom variablePrefix
  console.log('\nTest 4: Custom variablePrefix with important selector')
  try {
    const uno = await createGenerator({
      envMode: 'dev',
      presets: [
        presetWind4({
          important: '#app',
          variablePrefix: 'my-',
          preflights: { reset: false },
        }),
      ],
    })
    const { css } = await uno.generate('text-red', { preflights: false })
    
    const hasCustomProperty = css.includes('@property --my-text-opacity')
    const notWrapped = !css.includes('#app :is(@property')
    const usesCustomVar = css.includes('var(--my-text-opacity)')
    
    if (hasCustomProperty && notWrapped && usesCustomVar) {
      console.log('  ✅ PASS - Custom variable prefix works correctly')
      passCount++
    } else {
      console.log('  ❌ FAIL')
      console.log('    - Has custom @property:', hasCustomProperty)
      console.log('    - Not wrapped:', notWrapped)
      console.log('    - Uses custom var:', usesCustomVar)
      failCount++
    }
  } catch (e) {
    console.log('  ❌ ERROR:', e.message)
    failCount++
  }
  
  // Test 5: Multiple color utilities
  console.log('\nTest 5: Multiple color utilities generating multiple @properties')
  try {
    const uno = await createGenerator({
      envMode: 'dev',
      presets: [
        presetWind4({
          important: '#app',
          preflights: { reset: false },
        }),
      ],
    })
    const { css } = await uno.generate('text-red bg-blue border-green ring-yellow', { preflights: false })
    
    const properties = css.match(/@property --un-[a-z-]+/g) || []
    const invalidWrappings = css.includes('#app :is(@property')
    
    if (properties.length >= 4 && !invalidWrappings) {
      console.log(`  ✅ PASS - ${properties.length} properties generated, none wrapped`)
      passCount++
    } else {
      console.log('  ❌ FAIL')
      console.log('    - Properties found:', properties.length)
      console.log('    - Has invalid wrappings:', invalidWrappings)
      failCount++
    }
  } catch (e) {
    console.log('  ❌ ERROR:', e.message)
    failCount++
  }
  
  // Test 6: Combined options (important + variablePrefix + prefix)
  console.log('\nTest 6: All options combined')
  try {
    const uno = await createGenerator({
      envMode: 'dev',
      presets: [
        presetWind4({
          important: '#__nuxt',
          variablePrefix: 'uno-',
          prefix: 'u-',
          preflights: { reset: false },
        }),
      ],
    })
    const { css } = await uno.generate('u-text-red u-bg-blue', { preflights: false })
    
    const hasCustomProperty = css.includes('@property --uno-text-opacity')
    const notWrapped = !css.includes('#__nuxt :is(@property')
    const usesCustomVar = css.includes('var(--uno-text-opacity)')
    const selectorWrapped = css.includes('#__nuxt :is(.u-text-red)')
    
    if (hasCustomProperty && notWrapped && usesCustomVar && selectorWrapped) {
      console.log('  ✅ PASS - All options work together correctly')
      passCount++
    } else {
      console.log('  ❌ FAIL')
      console.log('    - Has custom @property:', hasCustomProperty)
      console.log('    - Not wrapped:', notWrapped)
      console.log('    - Uses custom var:', usesCustomVar)
      console.log('    - Selector wrapped:', selectorWrapped)
      failCount++
    }
  } catch (e) {
    console.log('  ❌ ERROR:', e.message)
    failCount++
  }
  
  console.log('\n' + '='.repeat(60))
  console.log(`RESULTS: ${passCount} passed, ${failCount} failed`)
  if (failCount === 0) {
    console.log('\n✅ ALL TESTS PASSED!')
    console.log('\nThe fix successfully addresses the issue:')
    console.log('  • @property declarations are never wrapped with important selector')
    console.log('  • @property declarations never have !important added')
    console.log('  • @property declarations respect custom variable prefixes')
    console.log('  • Regular selectors are correctly wrapped with important selector')
    console.log('  • Regular CSS properties correctly have !important when using important: true')
    console.log('  • All options (important, variablePrefix, prefix) work together')
  } else {
    console.log('\n❌ SOME TESTS FAILED - Please review the results above')
  }
  console.log('='.repeat(60) + '\n')
}

runTests()
EOF

+

+    expect(css).not.toContain('#app :is(@property')
+    expect(css).toContain('@property --un-text-opacity')
+    expect(css).toContain('@property --un-bg-opacity')
+    
+    // Check that regular selectors are wrapped
+    expect(css).toContain('#app :is(.text-red)')
+    expect(css).toContain('#app :is(.text-opacity-50)')
+    expect(css).toContain('#app :is(.dark .dark\\:bg-blue)')
+
+    await expect(css).toMatchFileSnapshot('./assets/output/preset-wind4-important-string.css')
+  })
+
+  it('important with true', async () => {
+    const uno = await createGenerator({
+      envMode: 'dev',
+      presets: [
+        presetWind4({
+          important: true,
+          preflights: { reset: false },
+        }),
+      ],
+    })
+
+    const { css } = await uno.generate([
+      'text-opacity-50',
+      'text-red',
+    ].join(' '), { preflights: false })
+
+    // Check that @property declarations don't have !important
+    const propertySection = css.split('/* layer: properties */')[1]?.split('/* layer:')[0] || ''
+    expect(propertySection).not.toContain('!important')
+    
+    // Check that regular CSS has !important
+    expect(css).toContain('color:color-mix(in srgb, var(--colors-red-DEFAULT) var(--un-text-opacity), transparent)')
+    expect(css).toContain('!important')
+
+    await expect(css).toMatchFileSnapshot('./assets/output/preset-wind4-important-true.css')
+  })

+import { createGenerator } from '@unocss/core'
+import presetWind4 from '@unocss/preset-wind4'
+
+async function testImportantWithVarPrefix() {
+  console.log('\n=== Testing important with custom variablePrefix ===\n')
+  
+  const uno = await createGenerator({
+    envMode: 'dev',
+    presets: [
+      presetWind4({
+        important: '#app',
+        variablePrefix: 'my-',
+        preflights: { reset: false },
+      }),
+    ],
+  })
+
+  const { css } = await uno.generate('text-red text-opacity-50', { preflights: false })
+  
+  console.log('Generated CSS:')
+  console.log(css)
+  console.log('\n')
+  
+  console.log('--- Validation ---')
+  
+  // Check that @property uses custom prefix
+  const hasCustomPrefixProperty = css.includes('@property --my-text-opacity')
+  console.log('✓ Has @property with custom prefix (--my-text-opacity):', hasCustomPrefixProperty)
+  
+  // Check that @property is not wrapped
+  const hasInvalidWrapping = css.includes('#app :is(@property')
+  console.log('✓ @property not wrapped with important selector:', !hasInvalidWrapping)
+  
+  // Check that CSS uses custom prefix in var()
+  const usesCustomPrefix = css.includes('var(--my-text-opacity)')
+  console.log('✓ CSS uses custom prefix in var():', usesCustomPrefix)
+  
+  // Check that regular selectors are wrapped
+  const hasWrappedSelectors = css.includes('#app :is(.text-red)')
+  console.log('✓ Regular selectors are wrapped:', hasWrappedSelectors)
+  
+  if (hasCustomPrefixProperty && !hasInvalidWrapping && usesCustomPrefix && hasWrappedSelectors) {
+    console.log('\n✅ All validations passed!')
+  } else {
+    console.log('\n❌ Some validations failed!')
+  }
+}
+
+async function testImportantWithPrefix() {
+  console.log('\n=== Testing important with utility prefix ===\n')
+  
+  const uno = await createGenerator({
+    envMode: 'dev',
+    presets: [
+      presetWind4({
+        important: '#app',
+        prefix: 'tw-',
+        preflights: { reset: false },
+      }),
+    ],
+  })
+
+  const { css } = await uno.generate('tw-text-red tw-text-opacity-50', { preflights: false })
+  
+  console.log('Generated CSS (excerpt):')
+  const lines = css.split('\n').slice(0, 10)
+  lines.forEach(line => console.log(line))
+  console.log('...\n')
+  
+  console.log('--- Validation ---')
+  
+  // Check that @property is not wrapped
+  const hasInvalidWrapping = css.includes('#app :is(@property')
+  console.log('✓ @property not wrapped with important selector:', !hasInvalidWrapping)
+  
+  // Check that regular selectors use prefix
+  const hasWrappedPrefixedSelectors = css.includes('#app :is(.tw-text-red)')
+  console.log('✓ Prefixed selectors are wrapped:', hasWrappedPrefixedSelectors)
+  
+  if (!hasInvalidWrapping && hasWrappedPrefixedSelectors) {
+    console.log('\n✅ All validations passed!')
+  } else {
+    console.log('\n❌ Some validations failed!')
+  }
+}
+
+async function testMultipleOptions() {
+  console.log('\n=== Testing with multiple options combined ===\n')
+  
+  const uno = await createGenerator({
+    envMode: 'dev',
+    presets: [
+      presetWind4({
+        important: '#__nuxt',
+        variablePrefix: 'uno-',
+        prefix: 'u-',
+        preflights: { reset: false },
+      }),
+    ],
+  })
+
+  const { css } = await uno.generate('u-text-red u-bg-blue', { preflights: false })
+  
+  console.log('Generated CSS (excerpt):')
+  const lines = css.split('\n').slice(0, 10)
+  lines.forEach(line => console.log(line))
+  console.log('...\n')
+  
+  console.log('--- Validation ---')
+  
+  // Check that @property uses custom variable prefix
+  const hasCustomVarPrefix = css.includes('@property --uno-text-opacity')
+  console.log('✓ @property uses custom variable prefix (--uno-):', hasCustomVarPrefix)
+  
+  // Check that @property is not wrapped
+  const hasInvalidWrapping = css.includes('#__nuxt :is(@property')
+  console.log('✓ @property not wrapped with important selector:', !hasInvalidWrapping)
+  
+  // Check that CSS uses custom variable prefix
+  const usesCustomVarPrefix = css.includes('var(--uno-text-opacity)')
+  console.log('✓ CSS uses custom variable prefix:', usesCustomVarPrefix)
+  
+  // Check that regular selectors use utility prefix and are wrapped
+  const hasWrappedPrefixedSelectors = css.includes('#__nuxt :is(.u-text-red)')
+  console.log('✓ Prefixed selectors are wrapped with important:', hasWrappedPrefixedSelectors)
+  
+  if (hasCustomVarPrefix && !hasInvalidWrapping && usesCustomVarPrefix && hasWrappedPrefixedSelectors) {
+    console.log('\n✅ All validations passed!')
+  } else {
+    console.log('\n❌ Some validations failed!')
+  }
+}
+
+async function runAllTests() {
+  await testImportantWithVarPrefix()
+  await testImportantWithPrefix()
+  await testMultipleOptions()
+  
+  console.log('\n=== All combination tests completed ===\n')
+}
+
+runAllTests()

+import { createGenerator } from '@unocss/core'
+import presetWind4 from '@unocss/preset-wind4'
+
+async function testVariousImportantSelectors() {
+  console.log('\n=== Testing various important selectors ===\n')
+  
+  const selectors = ['#app', '#__nuxt', '.main-wrapper', '#root']
+  
+  for (const selector of selectors) {
+    console.log(`Testing with important: "${selector}"`)
+    
+    const uno = await createGenerator({
+      envMode: 'dev',
+      presets: [
+        presetWind4({
+          important: selector,
+          preflights: { reset: false },
+        }),
+      ],
+    })
+
+    const { css } = await uno.generate('text-red bg-blue border-green', { preflights: false })
+    
+    // Check that @property declarations are not wrapped
+    const hasInvalidPropertyWrapping = css.includes(`${selector} :is(@property`)
+    const propertyDeclarations = css.match(/@property --un-[a-z-]+/g) || []
+    
+    if (hasInvalidPropertyWrapping) {
+      console.log(`  ❌ FAIL: @property declarations are wrapped with "${selector}"`)
+    } else if (propertyDeclarations.length > 0) {
+      console.log(`  ✓ PASS: ${propertyDeclarations.length} @property declarations are not wrapped`)
+    } else {
+      console.log(`  ⚠ WARNING: No @property declarations found`)
+    }
+    
+    // Check that regular selectors are wrapped
+    const hasWrappedSelectors = css.includes(`${selector} :is(.text-red)`)
+    if (hasWrappedSelectors) {
+      console.log(`  ✓ PASS: Regular selectors are properly wrapped`)
+    } else {
+      console.log(`  ❌ FAIL: Regular selectors are not wrapped`)
+    }
+    console.log('')
+  }
+}
+
+async function testPropertiesLayerWithVariousUtilities() {
+  console.log('\n=== Testing properties layer with various utilities ===\n')
+  
+  const uno = await createGenerator({
+    envMode: 'dev',
+    presets: [
+      presetWind4({
+        important: '#app',
+        preflights: { reset: false },
+      }),
+    ],
+  })
+
+  const utilities = [
+    // Color utilities
+    'text-red', 'text-opacity-50',
+    'bg-blue', 'bg-opacity-75',
+    'border-green', 'border-opacity-25',
+    // Shadow utilities
+    'text-shadow-red',
+    'shadow-red',
+    // Ring utilities
+    'ring-red', 'ring-opacity-50',
+    // Decoration utilities
+    'decoration-red',
+  ]
+
+  const { css } = await uno.generate(utilities.join(' '), { preflights: false })
+  
+  // Extract all @property declarations
+  const propertyMatches = css.match(/@property[^{]+\{[^}]+\}/g) || []
+  
+  console.log(`Total @property declarations: ${propertyMatches.length}`)
+  
+  // Check that none of them are wrapped with the important selector
+  const invalidProperties = propertyMatches.filter(prop => prop.includes('#app :is('))
+  
+  if (invalidProperties.length > 0) {
+    console.log(`❌ FAIL: ${invalidProperties.length} properties are incorrectly wrapped`)
+    invalidProperties.forEach(prop => {
+      console.log(`  - ${prop.substring(0, 60)}...`)
+    })
+  } else {
+    console.log('✓ PASS: All @property declarations are valid')
+  }
+  
+  // Check that all properties have proper syntax
+  const propertiesWithSyntax = propertyMatches.filter(prop => prop.includes('syntax:'))
+  console.log(`Properties with syntax: ${propertiesWithSyntax.length}/${propertyMatches.length}`)
+  
+  if (propertiesWithSyntax.length === propertyMatches.length) {
+    console.log('✓ PASS: All @property declarations have proper syntax definition')
+  } else {
+    console.log('❌ FAIL: Some @property declarations are missing syntax')
+  }
+  
+  console.log('')
+}
+
+async function testBothImportantModes() {
+  console.log('\n=== Testing both important modes (true vs selector) ===\n')
+  
+  // Test with important: true
+  const unoTrue = await createGenerator({
+    envMode: 'dev',
+    presets: [
+      presetWind4({
+        important: true,
+        preflights: { reset: false },
+      }),
+    ],
+  })
+
+  const { css: cssTrue } = await unoTrue.generate('text-red text-opacity-50', { preflights: false })
+  
+  console.log('Testing important: true')
+  
+  // Check that @property doesn't have !important
+  const propertiesSection = cssTrue.split('/* layer: properties */')[1]?.split('/* layer:')[0] || ''
+  const hasImportantInProperties = propertiesSection.includes('!important')
+  
+  if (hasImportantInProperties) {
+    console.log('  ❌ FAIL: @property declarations have !important')
+  } else {
+    console.log('  ✓ PASS: @property declarations do not have !important')
+  }
+  
+  // Check that regular CSS has !important
+  const defaultSection = cssTrue.split('/* layer: default */')[1] || ''
+  const hasImportantInDefault = defaultSection.includes('!important')
+  
+  if (hasImportantInDefault) {
+    console.log('  ✓ PASS: Default layer has !important')
+  } else {
+    console.log('  ❌ FAIL: Default layer does not have !important')
+  }
+  
+  // Test with important: '#app'
+  const unoSelector = await createGenerator({
+    envMode: 'dev',
+    presets: [
+      presetWind4({
+        important: '#app',
+        preflights: { reset: false },
+      }),
+    ],
+  })
+
+  const { css: cssSelector } = await unoSelector.generate('text-red text-opacity-50', { preflights: false })
+  
+  console.log('\nTesting important: "#app"')
+  
+  // Check that @property is not wrapped
+  const hasInvalidPropertyWrapping = cssSelector.includes('#app :is(@property')
+  
+  if (hasInvalidPropertyWrapping) {
+    console.log('  ❌ FAIL: @property declarations are wrapped with selector')
+  } else {
+    console.log('  ✓ PASS: @property declarations are not wrapped')
+  }
+  
+  // Check that regular selectors are wrapped
+  const hasWrappedSelectors = cssSelector.includes('#app :is(.text-red)')
+  
+  if (hasWrappedSelectors) {
+    console.log('  ✓ PASS: Regular selectors are wrapped with important selector')
+  } else {
+    console.log('  ❌ FAIL: Regular selectors are not wrapped')
+  }
+  
+  console.log('')
+}
+
+async function runAllTests() {
+  await testVariousImportantSelectors()
+  await testPropertiesLayerWithVariousUtilities()
+  await testBothImportantModes()
+  
+  console.log('\n=== All tests completed ===\n')
+}
+
+runAllTests()
